[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPDF parsing pipeline.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **What the issue is**  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer execution did not complete within the allotted time and triggered a [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlibFuzzer timeout. The thread dump shows the “main” thread in a RUNNABLE state, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrepeatedly invoking a native tracing callback as it processes a PDF input via [0m      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThere is no indication of an out-of-memory error or Java exception; rather, the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39missue is purely that the harness did not return.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Vulnerability type**  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  No explicit vulnerability type [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., crash, OOB, memory corruption[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmentioned. The issue manifests as a hang or severe performance degradation leading [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto a fuzzer timeout.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m221[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m222[0m[39m:                [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m223[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m224[0m[39m:            [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify the hang in the explicit‐array branch of Type1Parser.readEncoding  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The loop at lines [0m[1;36m217[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m224[0m[39m in [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/type1/Type1Parser.java  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m original[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     while [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             && [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"dup"[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 || [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"readonly"[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 || [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"def"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - On malformed or truncated input, `[0m[1;35mpeekKind[0m[1;39m([0m[39mToken.NAME[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` remains false [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindefinitely [0m[1;39m([0m[39mEOF yields no NAME tokens[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so the loop never terminates, causing the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer to hang.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Patch the loop to [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m check for EOF on each iteration and [0m[1;39m([0m[39mb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m bail out with an [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIOException when EOF is reached. This preserves existing behavior on valid fonts [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mwhere “dup”, “readonly” or “def” is eventually seen[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m but prevents infinite looping[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon malformed/truncated data.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Concrete patch outline [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno external APIs or harness changes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the original while‐condition with a robust loop:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m new[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         Token next = [0m[1;35mlexer.peekToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnext == null[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m EOF reached before finding dup/readonly/def → corrupt font[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Unexpected EOF while reading Type1 encoding [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mdictionary"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mnext.getKind[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == Token.NAME[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             String t = [0m[1;35mnext.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             if [0m[1;39m([0m[32m"dup"[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[39mt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[32m"readonly"[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[39mt[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[32m"def"[0m[1;35m.equals[0m[1;39m([0m[39mt[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                 break;[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mlexer.nextToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep the subsequent “dup…” loop and final `[0m[1;35mreadMaybe[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"readonly"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mread[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"def"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` unchanged so valid fonts parse exactly as before.[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Rationale[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Addresses the hang**: By explicitly breaking out or throwing on EOF, we [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavoid the infinite loop on malformed input that was causing the fuzzer timeout.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Preserves functionality**: No change to valid‐font parsing; only corrupted [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minputs now produce a clean IOException instead of hanging forever.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **No harness or fuzzing logic modifications**: We only change core parsing [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode in PDFBox’s Type1Parser; the Jazzer callback and fuzzing entry‐point remain [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntouched.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **No broad exception swallowing**: We throw a specific IOException right where[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe error occurs, making debugging easier and avoiding silent failures further down[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe pipeline.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Testing and side‐effect mitigation[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add unit tests feeding a truncated or completely invalid Type1 “Encoding” [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno “dup”[0m[35m/[0m[39m“def” markers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to verify that an IOException is thrown promptly [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather than looping.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify existing PDFBox Type1 font test suite still passes unchanged.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run the PDF text‐extraction fuzzer again to confirm no more timeouts on [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msimilar inputs.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Summary  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   This minimal patch prevents the infinite scanning loop in readEncoding for [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalformed Type1 fonts, directly resolving the fuzzer timeout. It is surgically [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfined to the Type1 font parser, avoids any harness or utility‐wide changes, and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproduces a clear error on corrupt data rather than hanging indefinitely.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
